<script type="text/javascript">
        jQuery( function ( $ ) {
            if ( ! ( window.Waypoint ) ) {
                // if Waypoint is not available, then we MUST remove our class from all elements because otherwise BGs will never show
                $('.lazyelementorbackgroundimages').removeClass('lazyelementorbackgroundimages');
                if ( window.console && console.warn ) {
                    console.warn( 'Waypoint library is not loaded so backgrounds lazy loading is turned OFF' );
                }
                return;
            } 
            var lazyelementorbackgroundimages_checkup = function () {
                $('.lazyelementorbackgroundimages').each( function () {
                    var $element = $( this );
                    new Waypoint({
                        element: $element.get( 0 ),
                        handler: function( direction ) {
                            //console.log( [ 'waypoint hit', $element.get( 0 ), $(window).scrollTop(), $element.offset() ] );
                            $element.removeClass('lazyelementorbackgroundimages');
                        },
                        offset: $(window).height()*1.5 // when item is within 1.5x the viewport size, start loading it
                    });
                } );
            };
            lazyelementorbackgroundimages_checkup();
            
            // also run an extra check after a swiper is in the viewport
            $('.swiper-container').each( function () {
                var $element = $( this );
                new Waypoint({
                    element: $element.get( 0 ),
                    handler: function () {
                        $element.find('.lazyelementorbackgroundimages').removeClass('lazyelementorbackgroundimages');
                    },
                    offset: $(window).height()*1.5 // when item is within 1.5x the viewport size, start loading it
                });
            } );
        });
    
</script>

<script>

function openMoto(evt, motoName) {
  var i, tabcontent, tablinks;
  tabcontent = document.getElementsByClassName("tabcontent");
  for (i = 0; i < tabcontent.length; i++) {
    tabcontent[i].style.display = "none";
  }
  tablinks = document.getElementsByClassName("tablinks");
  for (i = 0; i < tablinks.length; i++) {
    tablinks[i].className = tablinks[i].className.replace(" active", "");
  }
  document.getElementById(motoName).style.display = "flex";
  evt.currentTarget.className += " active";
};

</script>

			<script>
    
var getSystemsContainer = document.querySelector('#systemsContainer').querySelectorAll('.elementor-column');
var Yes = 'check';
var No = 'times';

function getIcon() {

for ( i=0; i<getSystemsContainer.length; i++ ) {
	var getSystemsId = getSystemsContainer[i].getAttribute('id');
	var getSystemAnswer = document.getElementById(getSystemsId).querySelector('.hideValue .elementor-text-editor').innerHTML;
	if ( getSystemAnswer === 'Si' ) {
		document.getElementById(getSystemsId).querySelector('.fa-icon').setAttribute('class', 'fa fa-' + Yes);
	} else if ( getSystemAnswer === 'No' ) {
		document.getElementById(getSystemsId).querySelector('.fa-icon').setAttribute('class', 'fa fa-' + No);
	}
}
    
}

window.onload = function(){
    getIcon();
}

</script>

    .hideValue {
        display: none !important;
        height: 0px !important;

    color: #52a136;
    }
    
    .fa-times {
        color: #949494;
    }

            var modeloClear = jQuery("#modelo").val();

            var numPlazosClear = jQuery("#num-plazos").val();
            //capturar parametro punto y asesor
            var puntoVenta = jQuery("#nombre-punto").val(getUrlVars()["punto_venta"]);
            var asesor = jQuery("#nombre-asesor").val(getUrlVars()["asesor"]);

           if (marcaClear == '' || modeloClear == '' ||  numPlazosClear == '' || cuotaClear == '' ) {
                var selectedMarca = jQuery("#auteco-brand").children("option:selected").text();
                jQuery("#marca").val(selectedMarca);

                var selectedVehiculo = jQuery("#auteco-vehiculos").children("option:selected").text();
                jQuery("#modelo").val(selectedVehiculo);

                var selectedPlazo = jQuery("#auteco-plazo-financiacion").children("option:selected").text();
                jQuery("#num-plazos").val(selectedPlazo);

                var selectedCuota = jQuery("#auteco-cuota").val();
                jQuery("#cuota-moto").val(selectedCuota);   
                    
                setTimeout(function(){
                    $(".mq-bank").each(function(){
                        var nombreAliado = jQuery(this).attr('id');
                        var cuotaAlido = jQuery(this).find('.table-cuotas p').text();

                        switch(nombreAliado) {
                            case 'sufi':
                                if (cuotaAlido != '') {
                                    jQuery("#cuota-sufi").val(cuotaAlido);
                                }else{
                                    jQuery("#cuota-sufi").val('Esta entidad puede financiar el monto ingresado');
                                }
                            break;

                            case 'finamiga':
                                if (cuotaAlido != '') {
                                    jQuery("#cuota-finamiga").val(cuotaAlido);
                                }else{
                                    jQuery("#cuota-finamiga").val('Esta entidad puede financiar el monto ingresado');
                                }
                            break;

                            case 'av villas':
                                if (cuotaAlido != '') {
                                    jQuery("#cuota-avvillas").val(cuotaAlido);
                                }else{
                                    jQuery("#cuota-avvillas").val('Esta entidad puede financiar el monto ingresado');
                                }
                            break;

                            case 'crediorbe':
                                if (cuotaAlido != '') {
                                    jQuery("#cuota-credi-orbe").val(cuotaAlido);
                                }else{
                                    jQuery("#cuota-credi-orbe").val('Esta entidad puede financiar el monto ingresado');
                                }
                            break;
                        }

                        

                    }); 
                }, 400);

                

                if (selectedMarca =='Selecciona una marca' || selectedVehiculo =="Selecciona una moto" || selectedPlazo =="Selecciona un plazo" || selectedCuota == "") {
                        jQuery(".mq-modal-wrapper").fadeIn();
                        //alert('marca vacia');
                }else{
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        jQuery( "#wpcf7-f551799-p540711-o1 form" ).submit();
                    }, 600);
                }

           }else{
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        jQuery( "#wpcf7-f551799-p540711-o1 form" ).submit();
                    }, 600);
           }
        });

        //capturar parametros desde url
        function getUrlVars() {
            var vars = {};
            var parts = window.location.href.replace(/[?&]+([^=&]+)=([^&]*)/gi, function(m,key,value) {
                vars[key] = value;
            });
            return vars;
        }

      });
 </script>
</div>
				</div>
				</div>

		<script>
			jQuery(document).ready(function() { 
				getLocation(); 
			});
			
			function getLocation() {
			  if (navigator.geolocation) {
				navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(showPosition);
			  } else {
				alert( "Geolocation is not supported by this browser.");
			  }
			}

			function showPosition(position) {
			//debugger;
			  console.log( "Latitude: " + position.coords.latitude +
			  " Longitude: " + position.coords.longitude);
			  jQuery.ajax({
				  type: "POST",
				  url:'/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php',
				  data: {action: "get_html_inventario_rows_clta", modelo: jQuery('#smodelo').val(), periodo: jQuery('#speriodo').val(), lat: position.coords.latitude, long: position.coords.longitude},
				  success: function(msg) {
					  jQuery("#gridInvent").html(msg.substr(0,(msg.length - 1)));
				  }
				});
			}
			
			/*jQuery('#cltaMap').on('click', function(event){

				}else{

					jQuery("#cltaMap").html("Ver en mapa");
